datasource</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active hover:font-semibold hover:underline href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-dev">tb dev</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active href="/docs/forward/dev-reference/commands/tb-job">tb job</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active pipe</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" aria-hidden="true" class="overflow-hidden transition-all" style="max-height:0"><div class="pt-2" style="padding-inline-start:16px"><ul class="space-y-2 border-l border-v-border"><li><a class="block class="text-sm font-semibold">Compliance</h5></a></li></ul></div><div class="border-y border-v-border mt-4 md:mt-auto md:border-b-0 py-2 px-2"><a class="py-2 px-3 flex gap-x-2 items-center rounded viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill="currentColor" d="M2.473 10.86a.7.7 0 0 0-.22-.14.67.67 0 0 0-.507 0 .7.7 0 0 0-.22.14.7.7 0 0 0-.14.22.67.67 0 0 0 .14.727q.099.089.22.14a.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .8.8 0 0 0 .22-.14.67.67 0 0 0 .14-.727.7.7 0 0 0-.14-.22m2.194-5.527H14A.667.667 0 1 0 14 4H4.667a.667.667 0 0 0 0 1.333M2.473 7.527a.67.67 0 0 0-.726-.14.8.8 0 0 0-.22.14.7.7 0 0 0-.14.22.63.63 0 0 0 0 .506q.05.123.14.22.097.09.22.14a.63.63 0 0 0 .506 0 .8.8 0 0 0 .22-.14.8.8 0 0 0 .14-.22.63.63 0 0 0 0-.506.7.7 0 0 0-.14-.22M14 7.333H4.667a.667.667 0 0 0 0 1.334H14a.667.667 0 1 0 0-1.334M2.473 bg-v-bg-button text-v-text-button border-transparent hover:border-v-border-button-hover inline-flex items-center"><div class="flex gap-2 items-center justify-center"><div>Start building</div></div></a><a class="text-button text-center py-1" href="https://ui.tinybird.co/login">Sign In</a></div></div></div></nav></aside><main class="w-full grow pt-6 pb-6 md:pt-8 sm:pb-8 md:max-w-[calc(100%_-var(--sidebar-width))]" data-pagefind-body=""><div class="hidden sm:block relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 "><nav aria-label="Breadcrumb" class="py-4 max-w-4xl md:px-4 mb-2"><ol class="flex items-center text-sm"><li><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/get-started/quickstarts">Home</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/monitoring">Monitor your data</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><span class="font-semibold">Monitor Kafka connectors</span></li></ol></nav></div><div class="relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]"><div class="max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative" role="main"><article><div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center justify-between gap-4 mb-6"><h1 id="monitor-kafka-to-clickhouse-connector-and-consumer-lag" class="t-h3" data-pagefind-weight="20.0">Monitor Kafka to ClickHouse® connector and consumer lag<a class="headerlink" href="#monitor-kafka-to-clickhouse-connector-and-consumer-lag" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h1><div class="flex-shrink-0 w-auto"><div class="relative inline-block w-auto" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="flex rounded-md overflow-hidden border border-v-border-02 hover:border-v-border-03 transition-colors"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm transition-colors min-w-[106px] text-v-text-01"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="w-4 h-4 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]"><path d="M14 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V8z"></path><path d="M14 2v6h6M16 13H8M16 17H8M10 9H8"></path></svg><span>Copy as MD</span></button><button class="flex items-center justify-center px-2 py-1.5 text-sm text-v-text-01 border-l border-v-border-02 min-w-[32px]" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" class="w-3 h-3 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]" style="margin-top:-4px;margin-left:-4px"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.1 11.41 4 6.995 4.745 6 8.1 9.795 11.454 6l.746.994z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><p>Tinybird&#x27;s Kafka connector automatically consumes data from Kafka topics and ingests it into ClickHouse® Data Sources. The connector features consumer autoscaling and multi-broker connectivity. The <code>tinybird.kafka_ops_log</code> <a href="/docs/forward/monitoring/service-datasources">Service Data Source</a> provides operational logs for monitoring your integration, tracking consumer lag, analyzing performance, and optimizing your connector configuration.</p><p>Use <code>kafka_ops_log</code> to monitor consumer lag, track throughput, identify errors, and analyze performance across your Data Sources. The connector&#x27;s serverless architecture automatically scales consumers based on load, and <code>kafka_ops_log</code> provides visibility into this autoscaling behavior along with error handling and debugging information.</p><p>Logs are retained for 30 days and include information about each partition, topic, and Data Source in your workspace. This supports analysis of partition assignment, rebalancing, and consumer group scaling behavior.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p><strong>New to the Kafka connector?</strong> If you&#x27;re setting up the Kafka connector for the first time, see the <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka">Kafka connector documentation</a> for setup instructions, configuration options, and troubleshooting. This monitoring guide focuses on operational monitoring once your connector is running.</p></div></div><h2 id="kafka-meta-columns-in-your-data-sources" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Kafka meta columns in your Data Sources<a class="headerlink" href="#kafka-meta-columns-in-your-data-sources" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>In addition to monitoring via <code>kafka_ops_log</code>, each Data Source connected to Kafka includes <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka#kafka-meta-columns">Kafka meta columns</a> that store metadata from Kafka messages. These columns are automatically added to your Data Source schema and can be used for analysis, debugging, and monitoring.</p><p>The available meta columns include:</p><ul><li><strong><code>__topic</code></strong>: The Kafka topic the message was read from</li><li><strong><code>__partition</code></strong>: The partition number the message was read from</li><li><strong><code>__offset</code></strong>: The message offset within the partition</li><li><strong><code>__timestamp</code></strong>: The timestamp of the Kafka message</li><li><strong><code>__key</code></strong>: The message key (if present)</li><li><strong><code>__value</code></strong>: The raw message value (if <code>KAFKA_STORE_RAW_VALUE</code> is set to <code>True</code>)</li><li><strong><code>__headers</code></strong>: Kafka headers as a Map (if <code>KAFKA_STORE_HEADERS</code> is set to <code>True</code>)</li></ul><h3 id="use-cases-for-kafka-meta-columns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Use cases for Kafka meta columns<a class="headerlink" href="#use-cases-for-kafka-meta-columns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Track message ordering and detect gaps</strong>: Use <code>__offset</code> to identify missing messages or gaps in your data ingestion. Compare consecutive offsets to detect when messages are skipped.</p><p><strong>Analyze distribution</strong>: Use <code>__partition</code> to understand how messages are distributed across partitions. This helps verify that your partition key design is working as expected and that messages are evenly distributed.</p><p><strong>Correlate with <code>kafka_ops_log</code></strong>: Join your Data Source with <code>kafka_ops_log</code> using <code>__partition</code> and <code>__offset</code> to correlate ingested messages with connector operations, helping you understand ingestion latency and identify bottlenecks.</p><p><strong>Message timestamp analysis</strong>: Compare <code>__timestamp</code> (Kafka message timestamp) with your Data Source&#x27;s ingestion timestamp to understand end-to-end latency from message production to ClickHouse ingestion.</p><p><strong>Debug with message keys</strong>: Use <code>__key</code> to track specific messages or understand how keys map to partitions, which is essential for partition key design optimization.</p><p><strong>Leverage headers for routing and tracing</strong>: If <code>KAFKA_STORE_HEADERS</code> is set to <code>True</code>, use <code>__headers</code> to access custom metadata, trace IDs, routing information, or other context stored in Kafka headers. This is useful for distributed tracing, A/B testing, or routing logic based on header values.</p><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Field</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>timestamp</code></td><td><code>DateTime</code></td><td>Date and time when the operation took place.</td></tr><tr><td><code>datasource_id</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>ID of your Data Source. The Data Source ID is consistent after renaming operations.</td></tr><tr><td><code>topic</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Kafka topic.</td></tr><tr><td><code>partition</code></td><td><code>Int16</code></td><td>Partition number, or <code>-1</code> for all partitions. Use this field to analyze partition assignment and identify which partitions are assigned to your consumer.</td></tr><tr><td><code>msg_type</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td><code>&#x27;info&#x27;</code> for regular messages, <code>&#x27;warning&#x27;</code> for issues related to the user&#x27;s Kafka cluster, deserialization or Materialized Views, and <code>&#x27;error&#x27;</code> for other issues.</td></tr><tr><td><code>lag</code></td><td><code>Int64</code></td><td>Number of messages behind for the partition. This is the difference between the high-water mark and the last commit offset. This is the primary metric for consumer lag monitoring.</td></tr><tr><td><code>processed_messages</code></td><td><code>Int32</code></td><td>Messages processed for a topic and partition.</td></tr><tr><td><code>processed_bytes</code></td><td><code>Int32</code></td><td>Amount of bytes processed.</td></tr><tr><td><code>committed_messages</code></td><td><code>Int32</code></td><td>Messages ingested for a topic and partition.</td></tr><tr><td><code>msg</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Information in the case of warnings or errors. Empty otherwise.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><p>The <code>tinybird.kafka_ops_log</code> Service Data Source includes operational metrics from your serverless Kafka connector. Each row represents a snapshot of the connector&#x27;s state for a specific partition at a point in time, providing visibility into autoscaling consumer behavior, error handling, and debugging information.</p><h2 id="monitor-consumer-lag" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Monitor consumer lag<a class="headerlink" href="#monitor-consumer-lag" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Consumer lag is the difference between the latest offset in a partition (high-water mark) and the last committed offset by your consumer. High lag values indicate that your consumer is falling behind the producer, which can lead to delayed data ingestion. With Tinybird&#x27;s serverless connector, consumer autoscaling automatically adjusts to handle increased load, but monitoring lag helps you understand when scaling occurs and verify that autoscaling is working effectively.</p><p>Monitoring consumer lag is critical for performance tuning. When lag increases, Tinybird&#x27;s autoscaling infrastructure automatically scales consumers to handle the load. The <code>kafka_ops_log</code> provides visibility into this autoscaling behavior, helping you understand partition assignment patterns and verify that your integration is performing optimally. For more details on consumer configuration, see the <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka">Kafka connector documentation</a>.</p><h3 id="find-current-consumer-lag-by-partition" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Find current consumer lag by partition<a class="headerlink" href="#find-current-consumer-lag-by-partition" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Get the most recent lag measurement for each partition:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    partition,
    lag,
    timestamp
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
  AND partition &gt;= 0
  AND msg_type = &#x27;info&#x27;
ORDER BY timestamp DESC
LIMIT 1 BY datasource_id, topic, partition
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="consumer-lag-trend-over-time" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Consumer lag trend over time<a class="headerlink" href="#consumer-lag-trend-over-time" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Track how lag changes over time to identify patterns and trends:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    toStartOfHour(timestamp) as hour,
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    partition,
    max(lag) as max_lag,
    avg(lag) as avg_lag
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
  AND partition &gt;= 0
  AND msg_type = &#x27;info&#x27;
GROUP BY hour, datasource_id, topic, partition
ORDER BY hour DESC, max_lag DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Rising lag trends may indicate that your current consumer group configuration cannot keep up with the message rate. This is particularly useful for understanding how Tinybird&#x27;s consumer autoscaling responds to varying load patterns.</p><h3 id="find-partitions-with-high-lag" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Find partitions with high lag<a class="headerlink" href="#find-partitions-with-high-lag" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Identify partitions that need immediate attention:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    partition,
    max(lag) as current_lag,
    timestamp
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
  AND partition &gt;= 0
  AND msg_type = &#x27;info&#x27;
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic, partition, timestamp
HAVING current_lag &gt; 10000
ORDER BY current_lag DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>High lag on specific partitions may indicate uneven message distribution, where some partitions receive more messages than others. This is valuable information for partition key design and scaling decisions.</p><h2 id="track-throughput-and-performance" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Track throughput and performance<a class="headerlink" href="#track-throughput-and-performance" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Throughput monitoring helps you understand how efficiently your connector is processing messages. This is essential for performance tuning and understanding how the autoscaling infrastructure responds to varying message rates.</p><h3 id="messages-processed-per-hour-by-topic" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Messages processed per hour by topic<a class="headerlink" href="#messages-processed-per-hour-by-topic" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Track message processing rates over time:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    toStartOfHour(timestamp) as hour,
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    sum(processed_messages) as total_messages,
    sum(processed_bytes) as total_bytes,
    sum(committed_messages) as total_committed
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
  AND msg_type = &#x27;info&#x27;
GROUP BY hour, datasource_id, topic
ORDER BY hour DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Use this to track throughput trends and identify peak processing periods. This data helps you understand how consumer autoscaling responds to load changes and supports capacity planning.</p><h3 id="processing-rate-comparison-across-partitions" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Processing rate comparison across partitions<a class="headerlink" href="#processing-rate-comparison-across-partitions" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Compare processing rates to identify bottlenecks:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    partition,
    sum(processed_messages) as total_processed,
    sum(committed_messages) as total_committed,
    count(*) as operation_count,
    sum(processed_messages) / count(*) as avg_messages_per_operation
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
  AND partition &gt;= 0
  AND msg_type = &#x27;info&#x27;
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic, partition
ORDER BY total_processed DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Uneven processing rates may indicate that you need to review your partition key design or adjust your partition assignment strategy.</p><h3 id="throughput-efficiency" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Throughput efficiency<a class="headerlink" href="#throughput-efficiency" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Compare processed messages to committed messages to understand your ingestion success rate:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    sum(processed_messages) as processed,
    sum(committed_messages) as committed,
    (sum(committed_messages) * 100.0 / sum(processed_messages)) as success_rate_pct
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
  AND msg_type = &#x27;info&#x27;
  AND processed_messages &gt; 0
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic
ORDER BY success_rate_pct ASC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>A low success rate indicates that messages are being processed but not successfully ingested into ClickHouse, which may point to schema issues, data quality problems, or configuration errors. The connector&#x27;s quarantine feature automatically handles problematic messages, and error details in <code>kafka_ops_log</code> help you debug and resolve issues. Learn more about <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/quarantine">Quarantine Data Sources</a>.</p><h2 id="monitor-errors-and-warnings" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Monitor errors and warnings<a class="headerlink" href="#monitor-errors-and-warnings" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Errors and warnings can indicate issues with your Kafka cluster connectivity, deserialization problems, Materialized View errors, or configuration issues. The serverless connector includes comprehensive error handling with quarantine for problematic messages. Regular monitoring of <code>kafka_ops_log</code> helps you catch and resolve issues before they impact your data pipeline. For troubleshooting guidance, see the <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka/troubleshooting">Kafka connector troubleshooting guide</a>.</p><h3 id="recent-errors-and-warnings" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Recent errors and warnings<a class="headerlink" href="#recent-errors-and-warnings" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>View all errors and warnings from your connector operations:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    timestamp,
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    partition,
    msg_type,
    msg,
    lag
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
  AND msg_type IN (&#x27;warning&#x27;, &#x27;error&#x27;)
ORDER BY timestamp DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Review these messages to identify patterns and root causes. Common issues include partition rebalancing events, deserialization failures, and connectivity problems.</p><h3 id="error-count-by-data-source-and-topic" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error count by Data Source and topic<a class="headerlink" href="#error-count-by-data-source-and-topic" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Identify which Data Sources or topics are experiencing the most issues:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    msg_type,
    count(*) as error_count
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
  AND msg_type IN (&#x27;warning&#x27;, &#x27;error&#x27;)
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic, msg_type
ORDER BY error_count DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This helps prioritize troubleshooting efforts and identify if specific topics or partitions are problematic.</p><h3 id="group-errors-by-message-type" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Group errors by message type<a class="headerlink" href="#group-errors-by-message-type" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Identify recurring issues and patterns:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    msg,
    msg_type,
    count(*) as occurrence_count,
    count(DISTINCT datasource_id) as affected_datasources
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 7 day
  AND msg_type IN (&#x27;warning&#x27;, &#x27;error&#x27;)
  AND msg != &#x27;&#x27;
GROUP BY msg, msg_type
ORDER BY occurrence_count DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This analysis helps you understand common failure modes in your connector.</p><h2 id="health-checks" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Health checks<a class="headerlink" href="#health-checks" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Regular health checks help you assess the overall status of your integration. These queries provide a comprehensive view of connector health, including consumer lag, throughput, and error rates. You can also set up automated <a href="/docs/forward/monitoring/health-checks">health checks</a> for continuous monitoring.</p><h3 id="connector-health-summary" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Connector health summary<a class="headerlink" href="#connector-health-summary" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Get a comprehensive health overview of all your connectors:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    max(lag) as max_lag,
    sum(processed_messages) as total_processed,
    sum(committed_messages) as total_committed,
    countIf(msg_type = &#x27;error&#x27;) as error_count,
    countIf(msg_type = &#x27;warning&#x27;) as warning_count,
    max(timestamp) as last_activity
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic
ORDER BY max_lag DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Use this for a quick assessment of your connector performance and to identify connectors that need attention.</p><h3 id="find-inactive-connectors" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Find inactive connectors<a class="headerlink" href="#find-inactive-connectors" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Find Data Sources that haven&#x27;t processed messages recently:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    max(timestamp) as last_activity,
    now() - max(timestamp) as time_since_last_activity
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 7 day
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic
HAVING time_since_last_activity &gt; INTERVAL 1 hour
ORDER BY time_since_last_activity DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Inactive connectors may indicate that the consumer has stopped, the topic has no new messages, or there&#x27;s a connectivity issue.</p><h2 id="partition-level-analysis" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Partition-level analysis<a class="headerlink" href="#partition-level-analysis" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Partition analysis helps you understand how your partition assignment strategy is working and identify partitions that may need attention. This analysis helps with scaling decisions and optimizing your partition key design.</p><h3 id="partition-performance-comparison" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Partition performance comparison<a class="headerlink" href="#partition-performance-comparison" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Compare performance metrics across all partitions:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    partition,
    max(lag) as max_lag,
    avg(lag) as avg_lag,
    sum(processed_messages) as total_messages,
    countIf(msg_type = &#x27;error&#x27;) as errors,
    countIf(msg_type = &#x27;warning&#x27;) as warnings
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
  AND partition &gt;= 0
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic, partition
ORDER BY max_lag DESC, errors DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This helps you understand if your partition assignment is balanced and whether you need to adjust your setup.</p><h3 id="lag-distribution-analysis" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Lag distribution analysis<a class="headerlink" href="#lag-distribution-analysis" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Understand the distribution of consumer lag across partitions:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    quantile(0.5)(lag) as median_lag,
    quantile(0.95)(lag) as p95_lag,
    quantile(0.99)(lag) as p99_lag,
    max(lag) as max_lag,
    min(lag) as min_lag
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
  AND partition &gt;= 0
  AND msg_type = &#x27;info&#x27;
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic
ORDER BY max_lag DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This helps identify if lag is evenly distributed or concentrated in specific partitions. Uneven lag distribution may indicate that you need to review your partition key design or consider rebalancing.</p><h2 id="alerting-queries" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Alerting queries<a class="headerlink" href="#alerting-queries" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Set up automated alerts based on these queries to catch issues early. These queries are designed to trigger alerts when critical conditions are met, helping you maintain reliable data pipelines. Combine these with <a href="/docs/forward/monitoring/health-checks">health checks</a> for comprehensive monitoring.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p><strong>Connect to monitoring tools</strong>: You can connect these monitoring queries to external alerting tools like Grafana, Datadog, PagerDuty, and Slack. Query the <a href="/docs/forward/work-with-data/publish-data/clickhouse-interface">ClickHouse HTTP interface</a> directly, or create API endpoints from these queries. For Prometheus-compatible tools, you can export queries in <a href="/docs/forward/work-with-data/publish-data/guides/consume-api-endpoints-in-prometheus-format">Prometheus format</a>. Configure your monitoring tools to poll these queries periodically and trigger alerts when thresholds are exceeded.</p></div></div><h3 id="high-consumer-lag-alert" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">High consumer lag alert<a class="headerlink" href="#high-consumer-lag-alert" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Alert when consumer lag exceeds a threshold:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    partition,
    lag,
    timestamp
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 5 minute
  AND partition &gt;= 0
  AND msg_type = &#x27;info&#x27;
  AND lag &gt; 50000
ORDER BY timestamp DESC
LIMIT 1 BY datasource_id, topic, partition
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>High lag indicates that your consumer is falling behind and may need scaling. With Tinybird&#x27;s consumer autoscaling, the infrastructure automatically handles increased load, but this alert helps you verify autoscaling effectiveness.</p><h3 id="error-rate-alert" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Error rate alert<a class="headerlink" href="#error-rate-alert" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Alert when the error rate exceeds a threshold:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    countIf(msg_type = &#x27;error&#x27;) as error_count,
    count(*) as total_operations,
    (countIf(msg_type = &#x27;error&#x27;) * 100.0 / count(*)) as error_rate_pct
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 15 minute
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic
HAVING error_rate_pct &gt; 5
ORDER BY error_rate_pct DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>High error rates indicate problems with your connector configuration, cluster connectivity, or data quality issues that need immediate attention.</p><h3 id="processing-stall-alert" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Processing stall alert<a class="headerlink" href="#processing-stall-alert" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Alert when no messages are being processed:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    max(timestamp) as last_activity,
    sum(processed_messages) as messages_in_window
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 10 minute
GROUP BY datasource_id, topic
HAVING messages_in_window = 0
ORDER BY last_activity DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This indicates that your consumer may have stopped, there&#x27;s a connectivity issue, or the topic has no new messages.</p><h2 id="combine-with-other-service-data-sources" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Combine with other Service Data Sources<a class="headerlink" href="#combine-with-other-service-data-sources" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>You can join <code>tinybird.kafka_ops_log</code> with other <a href="/docs/forward/monitoring/service-datasources">Service Data Sources</a> for deeper analysis. This supports comprehensive analysis that correlates connector operations with Data Source ingestion metrics. Learn more about all available <a href="/docs/forward/monitoring/service-datasources#tinybird-kafka-ops-log">Service Data Sources</a>.</p><h3 id="correlate-with-data-source-operations" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Correlate with Data Source operations<a class="headerlink" href="#correlate-with-data-source-operations" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Join Kafka operations log with <a href="/docs/forward/monitoring/service-datasources#tinybird-datasources-ops-log">Data Source operations log</a> to understand the complete pipeline from message consumption to ClickHouse ingestion:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    k.timestamp,
    k.datasource_id,
    k.topic,
    k.partition,
    k.processed_messages,
    k.committed_messages,
    d.rows as rows_in_datasource,
    d.elapsed_time
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log k
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT
        datasource_id,
        rows,
        elapsed_time,
        timestamp
    FROM tinybird.datasources_ops_log
    WHERE event_type = &#x27;append-kafka&#x27;
      AND timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
) d ON k.datasource_id = d.datasource_id
    AND toStartOfMinute(k.timestamp) = toStartOfMinute(d.timestamp)
WHERE k.timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
  AND k.msg_type = &#x27;info&#x27;
ORDER BY k.timestamp DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This helps you identify bottlenecks in the ingestion process and optimize your connector performance.</p><h3 id="analyze-ingestion-using-kafka-meta-columns" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Analyze ingestion using Kafka meta columns<a class="headerlink" href="#analyze-ingestion-using-kafka-meta-columns" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Use the <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka#kafka-meta-columns">Kafka meta columns</a> in your Data Sources to analyze ingestion patterns. For example, track message gaps by analyzing offset sequences:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    __partition,
    __topic,
    min(__offset) as min_offset,
    max(__offset) as max_offset,
    count(*) as message_count,
    max(__offset) - min(__offset) + 1 as expected_count,
    (max(__offset) - min(__offset) + 1) - count(*) as missing_messages
FROM your_kafka_datasource
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
GROUP BY __partition, __topic
HAVING missing_messages &gt; 0
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This helps identify if any messages were skipped during ingestion. You can also analyze distribution to verify your partition key design:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    __partition,
    count(*) as message_count,
    count(DISTINCT __key) as unique_keys,
    min(__timestamp) as first_message,
    max(__timestamp) as last_message
FROM your_kafka_datasource
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
GROUP BY __partition
ORDER BY __partition
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This shows how messages are distributed across partitions, helping you understand if your partition assignment is balanced.</p><h2 id="schema-evolution-monitoring" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Schema evolution monitoring<a class="headerlink" href="#schema-evolution-monitoring" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Monitor schema changes and their impact on ingestion:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    timestamp,
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    msg,
    count(*) as occurrence_count
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE msg_type = &#x27;warning&#x27;
  AND (msg LIKE &#x27;%schema%&#x27; OR msg LIKE &#x27;%deserialization%&#x27;)
  AND timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 24 hour
GROUP BY timestamp, datasource_id, topic, msg
ORDER BY occurrence_count DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This helps identify schema evolution issues and deserialization problems that may affect ingestion performance.</p><h2 id="performance-tuning-best-practices" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Performance tuning best practices<a class="headerlink" href="#performance-tuning-best-practices" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Based on monitoring data from <code>tinybird.kafka_ops_log</code>, follow these best practices:</p><ul><li><p><strong>Monitor consumer lag regularly</strong>: Set up alerts for high lag values to catch issues early. With Tinybird&#x27;s serverless architecture, consumer autoscaling automatically handles increased load, but monitoring lag helps you verify that autoscaling is working effectively.</p></li><li><p><strong>Track error patterns</strong>: Review error messages periodically to identify recurring issues. Common problems include partition assignment issues, deserialization failures, and connectivity problems.</p></li><li><p><strong>Compare partition performance</strong>: If one partition has significantly higher lag than others, investigate the cause. This may indicate uneven message distribution and the need to review your partition key design.</p></li><li><p><strong>Monitor throughput trends</strong>: Track processing rates over time to understand how the autoscaling infrastructure responds to varying message rates.</p></li><li><p><strong>Use time windows</strong>: Filter queries by recent time windows (for example, last hour, last 24 hours) to focus on current state and avoid analyzing stale data.</p></li><li><p><strong>Analyze partition assignment</strong>: Use partition-level metrics to understand if your partition assignment strategy is working effectively. Uneven partition loads may require rebalancing or adjustments to your setup.</p></li><li><p><strong>Optimize partition key design</strong>: If you see uneven lag distribution across partitions, consider reviewing your partition key design to ensure messages are distributed evenly.</p></li></ul><p>For detailed performance optimization strategies, see the <a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka/guides/performance-optimization">performance optimization guide</a>.</p><h2 id="next-steps" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Next steps<a class="headerlink" href="#next-steps" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="kafka-connector-documentation" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Kafka connector documentation<a class="headerlink" href="#kafka-connector-documentation" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><strong><a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka">Kafka connector guide</a></strong> - Complete setup, configuration, and troubleshooting guide</li><li><strong><a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka/troubleshooting">Troubleshooting guide</a></strong> - Common errors and solutions</li><li><strong><a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka/guides/performance-optimization">Performance optimization</a></strong> - Throughput tuning and best practices</li><li><strong><a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka/guides/partitioning-strategies">Partitioning strategies</a></strong> - Partition optimization</li><li><strong><a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka/guides/schema-management">Schema management</a></strong> - Schema evolution and data type mapping</li></ul><h3 id="monitoring-and-observability" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Monitoring and observability<a class="headerlink" href="#monitoring-and-observability" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><ul><li><strong><a href="/docs/forward/monitoring/service-datasources">Service Data Sources</a></strong> - Monitor ingestion performance</li><li><strong><a href="/docs/forward/monitoring/jobs">Workspace jobs</a></strong> - Additional pipeline observability</li></ul><h3 id="integrate-with-monitoring-tools" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Integrate with monitoring tools<a class="headerlink" href="#integrate-with-monitoring-tools" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Connect monitoring queries to Grafana, Datadog, PagerDuty, Slack, and other alerting systems by querying the <a href="/docs/forward/work-with-data/publish-data/clickhouse-interface">ClickHouse HTTP interface</a> directly. You can also create API endpoints from these queries, or export them in <a href="/docs/forward/work-with-data/publish-data/guides/consume-api-endpoints-in-prometheus-format">Prometheus format</a> for Prometheus-compatible tools.</p></article><div class="flex items-center justify-end h-10" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="italic text-caption"><span>Updated<!-- --> <time
